We
at

have
a
simple
mission:
to
facilitate
global
commerce.
Since
1993,
we
have
grown
to
become
the
world's
most
popular
currency
and
foreign
exchange
(fx, or forex)
site
by
developing
the
powerful
and
efficient
currency
services
that
the
new
global
economy
demands.
In
2002,
we
launched
XEtrade,
our
discount
on-line
foreign
exchange
payment
system.
XE.com
Forex
Speculation,
our
currency
speculation
service
that
allows
you
to
buy
and
sell
foreign
exchange
positions
in
real
time.-->

XE.com

and

to
premium
